<p>This article summarizes the events, album releases, and album release dates in <a href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title="Hip hop music">hip hop music</a> for the year 2013.</p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/T.I." title="T.I.">T.I.</a> completed his 10 year contract with <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Records" title="Atlantic Records">Atlantic Records</a>, and is seeking a deal around $75 million for him and his <a href="/wiki/Grand_Hustle_Records" title="Grand Hustle Records">Grand Hustle Records</a> artists.</li>
<li>On January 20, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Lupe_Fiasco" title="Lupe Fiasco">Lupe Fiasco</a> was removed from the stage by security after making anti-<a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Obama</a> comments in <a href="/wiki/Washington_D.C." title="Washington D.C." class="mw-redirect">Washington D.C.</a>, during <a href="/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Barack_Obama" title="Second inauguration of Barack Obama">Obama's second presidential inauguration</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On January 23, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Hit-Boy" title="Hit-Boy">Hit-Boy</a> confirmed he signed with <a href="/wiki/Interscope_Records" title="Interscope Records">Interscope Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On January 25, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Juelz_Santana" title="Juelz Santana">Juelz Santana</a> was sentenced to two years <a href="/wiki/Probation" title="Probation">probation</a> for threatening to kill his neighbor after his neighbor intervened and called the police when he heard Juelz assaulting his then girlfriend.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On January 28, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Rick_Ross" title="Rick Ross">Rick Ross</a> crashed his car in <a href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale" title="Fort Lauderdale" class="mw-redirect">Fort Lauderdale</a> after his vehicle was shot at in a <a href="/wiki/Drive_by_shooting" title="Drive by shooting" class="mw-redirect">drive by shooting</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span>[</span>4<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Jay-Z officially signed <a href="/wiki/Timbaland" title="Timbaland">Timbaland</a> to <a href="/wiki/Roc_Nation" title="Roc Nation">Roc Nation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On January 30, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Vado" title="Vado">Vado</a> confirmed he signed with <a href="/wiki/DJ_Khaled" title="DJ Khaled">DJ Khaled</a>'s <a href="/wiki/We_the_Best_Music_Group" title="We the Best Music Group">We the Best Music Group</a> label.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On February 8, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Rosenberg_(music_manager)" title="Paul Rosenberg (music manager)">Paul Rosenberg</a> confirmed <a href="/wiki/Eminem" title="Eminem">Eminem</a>'s eighth album will be released in 2013, post memorial day.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Drake won his first <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Best_Rap_Album" title="Grammy Award for Best Rap Album">Grammy Award for Best Rap Album</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2013_Grammy_Awards" title="2013 Grammy Awards" class="mw-redirect">2013 Grammy Awards</a> for <i><a href="/wiki/Take_Care_(album)" title="Take Care (album)">Take Care</a></i>. At the same night, Jay-Z and Kanye West would each take three Grammys; two for <a href="/wiki/Niggas_in_Paris" title="Niggas in Paris">Niggas in Paris</a> and one for <a href="/wiki/No_Church_in_the_Wild" title="No Church in the Wild">No Church in the Wild</a>.</li>
<li>On February 18, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Kollegah" title="Kollegah">Kollegah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Farid_Bang" title="Farid Bang">Farid Bang</a> topped the German album charts with their collabo album <i><a href="/wiki/Jung,_brutal,_gutaussehend_2" title="Jung, brutal, gutaussehend 2">Jung, brutal, gutaussehend 2</a></i> selling 80,000 copies in the release week. It is the highest number for a hip-hop album in Germany for the last five years.<sup id="cite_ref-JBG2_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JBG2-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>According to Billboard, <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Roc_Nation" title="Roc Nation">Roc Nation</a> imprint signed a “worldwide publishing administration deals with Warner/Chappell Music,” giving Jay-Z the rights back to his music post-<a href="/wiki/Def_Jam" title="Def Jam" class="mw-redirect">Def Jam</a> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Blueprint_3" title="The Blueprint 3">The Blueprint 3</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Watch_The_Throne" title="Watch The Throne" class="mw-redirect">Watch The Throne</a></i>) as well as future works, with most of his older catalog moving to the Warner umbrella within the year. A separate deal will put the past and future catalogs of Roc Nation’s stable of artists on the publisher’s roster immediately, including songwriters Philip Lawrence (<a href="/wiki/Bruno_Mars" title="Bruno Mars">Bruno Mars</a>, <a href="/wiki/Flo_Rida" title="Flo Rida">Flo Rida</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cee-Lo_Green" title="Cee-Lo Green" class="mw-redirect">Cee-Lo Green</a>), <a href="/wiki/S1_(producer)" title="S1 (producer)" class="mw-redirect">S1</a> (<a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a>, <a href="/wiki/Beyonce" title="Beyonce" class="mw-redirect">Beyonce</a>, <a href="/wiki/50_Cent" title="50 Cent">50 Cent</a>), Carmen Key (Flo Rida, <a href="/wiki/David_Guetta" title="David Guetta">David Guetta</a>), and British singer <a href="/wiki/Rita_Ora" title="Rita Ora">Rita Ora</a>, among others.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/C-Murder" title="C-Murder">C-Murder</a>'s appeal was rejected and he will remain in prison to serve out his life sentence due to a second degree murder committed in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Suge_Knight" title="Suge Knight">Suge Knight</a> has had two warrants for his arrest approved stating he can be arrested on the spot.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ja_Rule" title="Ja Rule">Ja Rule</a> has been released from prison for his possession of an illegal firearm charge but still has time to serve for tax evasion.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gunplay_(rapper)" title="Gunplay (rapper)">Gunplay</a> avoided his possible life sentence, and any jail time at all, due to the victim not cooperating and authenticating the video surveillance of him holding the victim up with a gun, and stealing a cellphone and gold chain.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On February 25, 2013, Atlanta rapper Young Vito, was acquitted of murdering <a href="/wiki/1017_Brick_Squad" title="1017 Brick Squad" class="mw-redirect">1017 Brick Squad</a> rapper <a href="/wiki/Slim_Dunkin" title="Slim Dunkin" class="mw-redirect">Slim Dunkin</a>. However, he was given 25 years for aggravated assault and possession of a firearm.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On March 1, 2013, former <a href="/wiki/No_Limit_Records" title="No Limit Records">No Limit Records</a> rapper <a href="/wiki/Awood_Johnson" title="Awood Johnson" class="mw-redirect">Mr. Magic</a> and his wife were killed in a car accident in Mississippi, their daughter who was with them at the time survived the crash. Magic was 37 years old at the time of his death.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Gunshots were fired near <a href="/wiki/French_Montana" title="French Montana">French Montana</a>'s tour bus when he was parked and chilling with fans and rapper <a href="/wiki/Meek_Mill" title="Meek Mill">Meek Mill</a> in Philadelphia, a 27 year old male was fatally shot in the stomach and was rushed to the hospital being pronounced DOA.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Method_Man" title="Method Man">Method Man</a> announced on stage that the <a href="/wiki/Wu-Tang_Clan" title="Wu-Tang Clan">Wu-Tang Clan</a> are working on a sixth studio album, that will be released this year to celebrate the 20th anniversary of the release of their debut album, <i><a href="/wiki/Enter_the_Wu-Tang_(36_Chambers)" title="Enter the Wu-Tang (36 Chambers)">Enter the Wu-Tang (36 Chambers)</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On March 12, 2013 <a href="/wiki/Lil_Wayne" title="Lil Wayne">Lil Wayne</a> suffered multiple seizures after shooting a music video in Los Angeles. He would be released later the same day.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup> Three days later he would be hospitalized again after another seizure, Thus causing <a href="/wiki/TMZ_(website)" title="TMZ (website)" class="mw-redirect">TMZ</a> to state he was in a medically <a href="/wiki/Induced_coma" title="Induced coma">induced coma</a> and being in critical condition. <a href="/wiki/YMCMB" title="YMCMB" class="mw-redirect">YMCMB</a> members <a href="/wiki/Mack_Maine" title="Mack Maine">Mack Maine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Birdman_(rapper)" title="Birdman (rapper)">Birdman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jay_Sean" title="Jay Sean">Jay Sean</a> and a slew of industry friends such as <a href="/wiki/T.I." title="T.I.">T.I.</a> would later deny these reports, and say he was in "good condition" and awake.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On March 14, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Keef" title="Chief Keef">Chief Keef</a> was released from a juvenile detention center after serving 60 days for violating his probation.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On March 16, 2013, Veteran California rapper <a href="/wiki/Tone_Loc" title="Tone Loc" class="mw-redirect">Tone Loc</a> collapsed on stage after finishing a song at the Bridge Bash concert in Des Moines, Iowa.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Cleveland Rapper <a href="/wiki/Machine_Gun_Kelly_(rapper)" title="Machine Gun Kelly (rapper)">Machine Gun Kelly</a> took home the 2013 <a href="/wiki/MtvU" title="MtvU">MtvU</a> "Woodie of the Year" award at the 2013 <a href="/wiki/MtvU" title="MtvU">MTV Woodie Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On March 22, 2013, Atlanta Police issued an arrest warrant for Radric Davis, aka <a href="/wiki/Gucci_Mane" title="Gucci Mane">Gucci Mane</a>, after he apparently assaulted a soldier with a champagne bottle.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On March 29, 2013, <a href="/wiki/Crypt_the_Warchild" title="Crypt the Warchild">Crypt the Warchild</a> of <a href="/wiki/OuterSpace" title="OuterSpace">OuterSpace</a> announced he was diagnosed with cancer.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sean_Combs" title="Sean Combs">Diddy</a> was announced to be the musical guest for <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania_29" title="WrestleMania 29">WrestleMania 29</a> which where he would perform a medley of songs on <a href="/wiki/Pay_per_view" title="Pay per view" class="mw-redirect">PPV</a> inside New Jersey's <a href="/wiki/MetLife_Stadium" title="MetLife Stadium">MetLife Stadium</a> on April 7.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kid_Cudi" title="Kid Cudi">Kid Cudi</a> revealed that he left <a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a>'s <a href="/wiki/GOOD_Music" title="GOOD Music">GOOD Music</a> record label, on good terms.</li>
<li>On April 3, 2013, at approximately 2 AM, <a href="/wiki/WWPR-FM" title="WWPR-FM">Power 105.1</a>'s host <a href="/wiki/DJ_Clue" title="DJ Clue" class="mw-redirect">DJ Clue</a> was arrested for drug possession and traffic violations.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Logic_(rapper)" title="Logic (rapper)">Logic</a> signs to <a href="/wiki/Def_Jam_Recordings" title="Def Jam Recordings">Def Jam Recordings</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurupt" title="Kurupt">Kurupt</a> announced that <a href="/wiki/Tha_Dogg_Pound" title="Tha Dogg Pound">Tha Dogg Pound</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bone_Thugs-N-Harmony" title="Bone Thugs-N-Harmony" class="mw-redirect">Bone Thugs-N-Harmony</a> are working on a collaboration album that will include all members of both groups along with <a href="/wiki/Snoop_Dogg" title="Snoop Dogg">Snoop Dogg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Soopafly" title="Soopafly">Soopafly</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On May 1, Chris Kelly of hip hop duo <a href="/wiki/Kris_Kross" title="Kris Kross">Kris Kross</a> died at the age of 34.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On May 3, record producer <a href="/wiki/AraabMuzik" title="AraabMuzik">AraabMuzik</a> was shot in an attempted robbery in his neighborhood, and taken to the hospital where he is recovering.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On May 6, 90s hip hop group <a href="/wiki/Naughty_By_Nature" title="Naughty By Nature" class="mw-redirect">Naughty By Nature</a> announced that they were splitting up.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On May 8, Gucci Mane announced <a href="/wiki/Chief_Keef" title="Chief Keef">Chief Keef</a> was officially signed to his <a href="/wiki/1017_Brick_Squad_Records" title="1017 Brick Squad Records">1017 Brick Squad Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span>[</span>31<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a> announced that his sixth studio album <i><a href="/wiki/Yeezus" title="Yeezus">Yeezus</a></i> would be released on June 18. <a href="/wiki/J._Cole" title="J. Cole">J. Cole</a> would move up the release date of his second album <i><a href="/wiki/Born_Sinner" title="Born Sinner">Born Sinner</a></i> to that same date.</li>
<li>On May 23, it was reported that rapper <a href="/wiki/Tim_Dog" title="Tim Dog">Tim Dog</a> might had faked his death in order to not pay back money after being convicted of fraud.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span>[</span>32<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On June 2, <a href="/wiki/Papoose_(rapper)" title="Papoose (rapper)">Papoose</a> "crashed" <a href="/wiki/WQHT" title="WQHT">Hot 97</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Summer_Jam" title="Summer Jam">Summer Jam</a> following Kendrick Lamar's set performing his single "Get At Me" with <a href="/wiki/Ron_Browz" title="Ron Browz">Ron Browz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On June 9, 2 Chainz was robbed at gunpoint in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a> of his phone and wallet. Two days later while boarding a flight from <a href="/wiki/LAX" title="LAX" class="mw-redirect">LAX</a>, TSA agents found that his checked bag contained marijuana and <a href="/wiki/Promethazine" title="Promethazine">promethazine</a>. He was arrested and booked on felony <a href="/wiki/Narcotics" title="Narcotics" class="mw-redirect">narcotics</a> possession.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On June 14, Kanye West's <i>Yeezus</i> leaked online in its entirety. It was the last of the June 18 album releases to leak as <i>Born Sinner</i> and <a href="/wiki/Mac_Miller" title="Mac Miller">Mac Miller</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Watching_Movies_with_the_Sound_Off" title="Watching Movies with the Sound Off">Watching Movies with the Sound Off</a></i> had leaked earlier in the month.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On June 16, through an advertisement for <a href="/wiki/Samsung" title="Samsung">Samsung</a> shown during the <a href="/wiki/2013_NBA_Finals" title="2013 NBA Finals">2013 NBA Finals</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> announced that he will release a new album titled <i><a href="/wiki/Magna_Carta_Holy_Grail" title="Magna Carta Holy Grail">Magna Carta Holy Grail</a></i> on July 4.</li>
<li>On June 20, <a href="/wiki/Dream_Chasers_Records" title="Dream Chasers Records" class="mw-redirect">Dream Chasers Records</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Lil_Snupe" title="Lil Snupe" class="mw-redirect">Lil Snupe</a> was murdered in <a href="/wiki/Winnfield,_Louisiana" title="Winnfield, Louisiana">Winnfield, Louisiana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Kanye West's sixth studio album Yeezus debuts at #1 on the Billboard 200 with 328,800 copies, beating out J. Cole's Born Sinner which debuted at #2 with 297,922 copies and Mac Miller's Watching Movies with the Sound Off which debuted at #3 with 101,795 copies.</li>
<li>On June 22, <a href="/wiki/Drake_(rapper)" title="Drake (rapper)">Drake</a> released four new songs, and announced the release date for his third album <i><a href="/wiki/Nothing_Was_the_Same" title="Nothing Was the Same">Nothing Was the Same</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On June 28, Meek Mill was ordered to take etiquette classes in order to tighten up on his social media skills and better articulate his business dealings, after some of his fans threatened his <a href="/wiki/Parole_Officer" title="Parole Officer" class="mw-redirect">PO</a> on Twitter.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On July 8, rapper <a href="/wiki/Wiz_Khalifa" title="Wiz Khalifa">Wiz Khalifa</a> officially married his girlfriend <a href="/wiki/Amber_Rose" title="Amber Rose">Amber Rose</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On July 25, <a href="/wiki/DJ_Khaled" title="DJ Khaled">DJ Khaled</a> publicly "proposed" to fellow <a href="/wiki/Cash_Money_Records" title="Cash Money Records">Cash Money</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Nicki_Minaj" title="Nicki Minaj">Nicki Minaj</a> via <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">MTV</a>. He supported his offer with a 10 karat diamond ring from Rafaello &amp; Co., valued at about $500,000.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup> However it was later revealed it was all a ploy to debut his new single "<a href="/wiki/I_Wanna_Be_with_You_(DJ_Khaled_song)" title="I Wanna Be with You (DJ Khaled song)">I Wanna Be with You</a>".</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On August 13, <a href="/wiki/Big_Sean" title="Big Sean">Big Sean</a> released a leftover track from his sophomore album <i><a href="/wiki/Hall_of_Fame_(Big_Sean_album)" title="Hall of Fame (Big Sean album)">Hall of Fame</a></i>, "<a href="/wiki/Control_(Big_Sean_song)" title="Control (Big Sean song)">Control</a>" which features <a href="/wiki/Kendrick_Lamar" title="Kendrick Lamar">Kendrick Lamar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jay_Electronica" title="Jay Electronica">Jay Electronica</a>. Lamar's verse caused controversy as he "called out" J. Cole, <a href="/wiki/Big_K.R.I.T." title="Big K.R.I.T.">Big K.R.I.T.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wale_(rapper)" title="Wale (rapper)">Wale</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pusha_T" title="Pusha T">Pusha T</a>, Meek Mill, <a href="/wiki/ASAP_Rocky" title="ASAP Rocky">ASAP Rocky</a>, Drake, Big Sean, Jay Electronica, <a href="/wiki/Tyler,_The_Creator" title="Tyler, The Creator">Tyler, The Creator</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mac_Miller" title="Mac Miller">Mac Miller</a> and called himself the "King of New York".<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup> Many rappers took offense to the lines without even being mentioned by name. Rappers including <a href="/wiki/Lupe_Fiasco" title="Lupe Fiasco">Lupe Fiasco</a>, <a href="/wiki/Papoose_(rapper)" title="Papoose (rapper)">Papoose</a>, <a href="/wiki/Joell_Ortiz" title="Joell Ortiz">Joell Ortiz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cassidy_(rapper)" title="Cassidy (rapper)">Cassidy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Riff_Raff_(rapper)" title="Riff Raff (rapper)">Riff Raff</a>, <a href="/wiki/Joe_Budden" title="Joe Budden">Joe Budden</a>, <a href="/wiki/ASAP_Ferg" title="ASAP Ferg">ASAP Ferg</a>, <a href="/wiki/JR_Writer" title="JR Writer" class="mw-redirect">JR Writer</a>, <a href="/wiki/King_L" title="King L">King L</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Mad_Rapper" title="The Mad Rapper" class="mw-redirect">The Mad Rapper</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mickey_Factz" title="Mickey Factz">Mickey Factz</a>, Mysonne, <a href="/wiki/Bizarre_(rapper)" title="Bizarre (rapper)">Bizarre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uncle_Murda" title="Uncle Murda">Uncle Murda</a>, Fred The Godson, and <a href="/wiki/B.o.B" title="B.o.B">B.o.B</a> all released a response or a diss song within a week.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On August 25, it was announced during the <a href="/wiki/2013_MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="2013 MTV Video Music Awards">2013 MTV Video Music Awards</a> that <a href="/wiki/Eminem" title="Eminem">Eminem</a> would release the sequel of the commercial and critically successful <i><a href="/wiki/The_Marshall_Mathers_LP" title="The Marshall Mathers LP">The Marshall Mathers LP</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Marshall_Mathers_LP_2" title="The Marshall Mathers LP 2">The Marshall Mathers LP 2</a></i> on November 5, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On August 26, <a href="/wiki/Fat_Joe" title="Fat Joe">Fat Joe</a> reported federal prison in Florida to serve a 4-month sentence for tax evasion.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On September 16, <a href="/wiki/Young_Money_Entertainment" title="Young Money Entertainment">Young Money Entertainment</a> president <a href="/wiki/Mack_Maine" title="Mack Maine">Mack Maine</a> was charged with sexual battery and assault in Oklahoma. According to court documents obtained by TMZ alleged that, Maine put his hand down one woman's shirt without her consent. Then while the women were trying to leave, Mack Maine reportedly held the door shut and also punched and broke one of the female's jaw.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On September 19, it was announced that the first theatrically-released <a href="/wiki/Tupac_Shakur" title="Tupac Shakur">Tupac Shakur</a> biopic will begin production in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On September 19, <a href="/wiki/Greeks" title="Greeks">Greek</a> rapper <a href="/wiki/Pavlos_Fyssas" title="Pavlos Fyssas" class="mw-redirect">Pavlos Fyssas</a> who went by the stage name Killah P, was stabbed to death. Riots broke out throughout <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a> due to the assumed political influences in the killing.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On September 27, former <a href="/wiki/UGK_Records" title="UGK Records" class="mw-redirect">UGK Records</a> artist, Ivory P was arrested on <a href="/wiki/Human_trafficking" title="Human trafficking">human trafficking</a> and kidnapping charges, for kidnapping a 19-year old woman to traffic out as <a href="/wiki/Escort_prostitute" title="Escort prostitute" class="mw-redirect">sexual escort</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On October 8, <a href="/wiki/Nipsey_Hussle" title="Nipsey Hussle">Nipsey Hussle</a> released his mixtape <i><a href="/wiki/Crenshaw_(mixtape)" title="Crenshaw (mixtape)">Crenshaw</a></i> for free online, and in a limited 1,000 physical copies for $100 each. He sold out all the copies earning over 100,000 dollars in one day.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On October 12, <a href="/wiki/The_Game_(rapper)" title="The Game (rapper)">The Game</a> following his official release from <a href="/wiki/Interscope_Records" title="Interscope Records">Interscope Records</a> signed to <a href="/wiki/Cash_Money_Records" title="Cash Money Records">Cash Money Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span>[</span>57<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On October 15, <a href="/wiki/Future_(rapper)" title="Future (rapper)">Future</a> was dropped off of <a href="/wiki/Drake_(rapper)" title="Drake (rapper)">Drake</a>'s third headlining tour <a href="/wiki/Would_You_like_a_Tour%3F" title="Would You like a Tour?">Would You like a Tour?</a> after he made negative comments about Drake and <a href="/wiki/Nothing_Was_the_Same" title="Nothing Was the Same">his album</a> in a <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_(magazine)" title="Billboard (magazine)">Billboard</a></i> interview. It was also reported he was demanding $1.5 million for lost wages, as he was set to get $40,000 per gig. He was subsequently replaced with <a href="/wiki/Jhen%C3%A9_Aiko" title="Jhené Aiko">Jhené Aiko</a> on every date of the tour. Two days later, Future rejoined the tour and drops the lawsuit.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58"><span>[</span>58<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>On November 7, Eminem became the first artist since <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">The Beatles</a>, to be the lead artist with four songs in the top 20 of the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> during the same week ("<a href="/wiki/The_Monster_(song)" title="The Monster (song)">The Monster</a>" at #3, "<a href="/wiki/Berzerk_(song)" title="Berzerk (song)">Berzerk</a>" at #15, "<a href="/wiki/Survival_(Eminem_song)" title="Survival (Eminem song)">Survival</a>" at #16, "<a href="/wiki/Rap_God" title="Rap God">Rap God</a>" at #17).<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60"><span>[</span>60<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On November 15, it was revealed that after Kendrick Lamar was named <i><a href="/wiki/GQ" title="GQ">GQ</a></i><span style="padding-left:0.1em;">'</span>s "Rapper of the Year" and interviewed for the issue, <a href="/wiki/Top_Dawg_Entertainment" title="Top Dawg Entertainment">Top Dawg Entertainment</a>'s CEO Anthony “Top Dawg” Tiffith took issue with the article and the interview, then pulling Kendrick Lamar from his performance at <i>GQ</i>'s annual Man Of The Year party that took place on, November 12, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span>[</span>61<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On November 22, <a href="/wiki/T.I." title="T.I.">T.I.</a> announced his signing to <a href="/wiki/Columbia_Records" title="Columbia Records">Columbia Records</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> has the most Grammy nominations for the <a href="/wiki/56th_Annual_Grammy_Awards" title="56th Annual Grammy Awards">56th Annual Grammy Awards</a> with 9. <a href="/wiki/Kendrick_Lamar" title="Kendrick Lamar">Kendrick Lamar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Macklemore" title="Macklemore">Macklemore</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Pharrell" title="Pharrell" class="mw-redirect">Pharrell</a> each have 7 nominations while <a href="/wiki/Drake_(rapper)" title="Drake (rapper)">Drake</a> has 5 nominations. Also, <a href="/wiki/T.I." title="T.I.">T.I.</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">Kanye West</a> each have 2 Grammy nominations.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Eminem" title="Eminem">Eminem</a> is now tied with the record of most Billboard Hot 100 #1's among rappers with <a href="/wiki/Sean_Combs" title="Sean Combs">Diddy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ludacris" title="Ludacris">Ludacris</a> with 5, with "<a href="/wiki/The_Monster_(song)" title="The Monster (song)">The Monster</a>" peaking at #1. <sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On December 17, <a href="/wiki/Pharrell" title="Pharrell" class="mw-redirect">Pharrell</a> signed to <a href="/wiki/Columbia_Records" title="Columbia Records">Columbia Records</a> as a solo artist and announced that he would release his second album on the label during 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On December 20, <a href="/wiki/Three_6_Mafia" title="Three 6 Mafia">Three 6 Mafia</a> member and <a href="/wiki/DJ_Paul" title="DJ Paul">DJ Paul</a>'s brother <a href="/wiki/Lord_Infamous" title="Lord Infamous">Lord Infamous</a> died from a heart attack.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On December 28, Grand Hustle Records and <a href="/wiki/Interscope_Records" title="Interscope Records">Interscope Records</a> artist <a href="/wiki/Doe_B" title="Doe B">Doe B</a> was shot and killed in his home state of <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On December 29, <a href="/wiki/Waka_Flocka_Flame" title="Waka Flocka Flame">Waka Flocka Flame</a>'s little brother and <a href="/wiki/Brick_Squad_Monopoly" title="Brick Squad Monopoly" class="mw-redirect">Brick Squad Monopoly</a> artist KayO Redd died from an apparent <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a> in Atlanta.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Highest-charting_songs">Highest-charting songs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Highest-charting songs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg/220px-Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg" width="220" height="141" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg/330px-Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg/440px-Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2934" data-file-height="1884" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis_at_Sasquatch_2011.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf7/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt="" /></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Macklemore_%26_Ryan_Lewis" title="Macklemore &amp; Ryan Lewis">Macklemore &amp; Ryan Lewis</a> released the hit singles "<a href="/wiki/Thrift_Shop_(song)" title="Thrift Shop (song)" class="mw-redirect">Thrift Shop</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Can%27t_Hold_Us" title="Can't Hold Us">Can't Hold Us</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Same_Love" title="Same Love">Same Love</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/White_Walls" title="White Walls">White Walls</a>" during 2013.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jay-Z_3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Jay-Z_3.jpg/220px-Jay-Z_3.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Jay-Z_3.jpg/330px-Jay-Z_3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Jay-Z_3.jpg/440px-Jay-Z_3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="3000" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jay-Z_3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf7/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt="" /></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Jay-Z" title="Jay-Z">Jay-Z</a> released the hit singles "<a href="/wiki/Holy_Grail_(Jay-Z_song)" title="Holy Grail (Jay-Z song)">Holy Grail</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/Tom_Ford_(song)" title="Tom Ford (song)">Tom Ford</a>" during 2013.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg/180px-Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg" width="180" height="221" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg/270px-Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg/360px-Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg 2x" data-file-width="999" data-file-height="1224" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Drake_at_Bun-B_Concert_2011.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf7/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt="" /></a></div>
During 2013, <a href="/wiki/Drake_(rapper)" title="Drake (rapper)">Drake</a> released the hit singles "<a href="/wiki/Started_from_the_Bottom" title="Started from the Bottom">Started from the Bottom</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/All_Me_(Drake_song)" title="All Me (Drake song)">All Me</a>", along with being featured on "<a href="/wiki/Fuckin%27_Problems" title="Fuckin' Problems">Fuckin' Problems</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Love_Me_(Lil_Wayne_song)" title="Love Me (Lil Wayne song)">Love Me</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Poetic_Justice_(song)" title="Poetic Justice (song)">Poetic Justice</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/No_New_Friends" title="No New Friends">No New Friends</a>".</div>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Highest_first-week_sales">Highest first-week sales</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Highest first-week sales">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg/180px-Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg" width="180" height="288" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg/270px-Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg/360px-Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg 2x" data-file-width="371" data-file-height="594" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eminem_DJ_Hero.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"><img src="//bits.wikimedia.org/static-1.24wmf7/skins/common/images/magnify-clip.png" width="15" height="11" alt="" /></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Eminem" title="Eminem">Eminem</a>'s eighth studio album <i><a href="/wiki/The_Marshall_Mathers_LP_2" title="The Marshall Mathers LP 2">The Marshall Mathers LP 2</a></i> sold 793,000 copies in the United States during its first week of release.</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Highest_critically_reviewed_albums_.28Metacritic.29">Highest critically reviewed albums (Metacritic)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_in_hip_hop_music&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Highest critically reviewed albums (Metacritic)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg/220px-Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg" width="220" height="246" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg/330px-Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg/440px-Kanye_West_Lollapalooza_Chile_2011_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1056" data-file-height="1183" /></a>
